<div id="review_327774369" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/327774369" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/327774369?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer327774369" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17993825140972460062"><b>4.5 Beautifully disturbing stars...</b><br/><br/>This book, if nothing else, makes you honestly and completely 'FEEL'-- horror, disgust, pity, anger, lust, shame, hatred, love--whichever emotion it ignites in you, I promise, you'll feel it to the millionth degree! There is nothing romantic about this story; at least not in the traditional sense, anyway. It's gritty and crude and created not to please, but to ignite raw, uninhibited emotions that will leave you feeling exhausted... But the fact is, no other bo</span>
  <span id="freeText17993825140972460062" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Beautifully disturbing stars...</b><br><br>This book, if nothing else, makes you honestly and completely 'FEEL'-- horror, disgust, pity, anger, lust, shame, hatred, love--whichever emotion it ignites in you, I promise, you'll feel it to the millionth degree! There is nothing romantic about this story; at least not in the traditional sense, anyway. It's gritty and crude and created not to please, but to ignite raw, uninhibited emotions that will leave you feeling exhausted... But the fact is, no other book has ever evoked such an array of gut-wrenching emotions or left me feeling almost violated just for having read it quite like this one has.<br><br><b>
  <i>He was my tormentor and my solace; the creator of the dark and the light within.</i>
</b><br><br>Caleb is not about love. He's about power and is living his life for a revenge that he will go to any extent to obtain. The sweet, broken, and innocent Livvie unluckily becomes his tool for this intricate, sinister plan of revenge. He captures her and sets forth towards his goal of turning her into a pleasure slave. It all seems simple and by the book; break her down and build her back up into the perfect submissive that no captor will be able to resist. But Caleb didn't plan on feeling things for Livvie he never thought he was capable of feeling. <br><br>Don't let me confuse you. Caleb does NOT go from frog to prince and live happily ever after. Not by a long shot. He is an abusive, callous monster. His behavior towards Livvie was vomit-inducing and I spent the majority of the book detesting him. But then there were conflicting, tender moments where he displayed a true conscience. Moments where I was able to sympathize with his torturous childhood, and somehow understand him. Granted, these moments were fleeting and quickly swallowed up by more insanity, but they <i>were</i> there. Which consequently left me all the more frustrated and confused. <br><br>Once I diffused the mental war I was having of bad Caleb VS. <i>slightly less</i> bad Caleb... I felt much more at ease with the story. Livvie was a lovable character whose ferocious strength surprised me. Her backstory was heartbreaking and she was very broken because of it. Caleb's childhood was even more heartbreaking and to say that he was damaged from it would be a severe understatement. I know that some readers ended up adoring Caleb, but it just hasn't happened yet for me. However, I saw the story for what it was and did not need to fall in love with Caleb to appreciate it. <br><br>This book was gripping and flawlessly written. It immediately ripped me out of my comfort zone, made me feel awkwardly amazed, and caused me to question my beliefs and morals. It made me search for kindness in places I'd least expect to find it. It has opened my eyes to a horrible world that I fortunately know little about and I fully believe that this was the story's true intent. <br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Dark Erotica<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Maximum/graphic<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Scarce to none. Twisted and unconventional.<br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Cold, detached, disturbed hero. Abused, secluded, withdrawn heroine.<br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Focused intensely on sex slavery and psychological manipulation. Will bulldoze your emotions.<br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Phenomenal. Gripping. Raw. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> First person: Heroine<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> Yes. Next installment available.<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Follow up<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_433215655" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/433215655" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/433215655?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer433215655" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2630996574946249186"><br/><b>WOW WOW WOW WOW...just, WOW.</b><br/><br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/636282.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/><br/><b>Speechless</b>... that's how I felt after reading this story...<br/><br/>It's <b>dark, twisted and disturbing on so many levels</b> but still I could NOT stop reading it!!! At times I really hated reading some of the things that happened, but the story was so addictive and intense that I couldn't help but love, love, love it!!!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"He was the monster no one thought to look for in the light of day. It was a common mistake. People often believed they were safer in the light, thinkin</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText2630996574946249186" style="display:none"><br><b>WOW WOW WOW WOW...just, WOW.</b><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/636282.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><b>Speechless</b>... that's how I felt after reading this story...<br><br>It's <b>dark, twisted and disturbing on so many levels</b> but still I could NOT stop reading it!!! At times I really hated reading some of the things that happened, but the story was so addictive and intense that I couldn't help but love, love, love it!!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"He was the monster no one thought to look for in the light of day. It was a common mistake. People often believed they were safer in the light, thinking monsters only came out at night."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>When we first meet Caleb, that's exactly what he is; a monster who has set his eyes on the young, poor girl named Olivia Ruiz. As a little boy, Caleb was forced into the world of pleasure slaves by the corrupt Russian business man Demitri Balk. The young boy has to suffer through a lot of horrible experiences because of this man and that is why Caleb decides to take revenge on the person who ruined his life. To succeed in his plan of revenge he wants to use Olivia, train her as a pleasure slave and sell her to Demitri to get as close as possible to his biggest enemy. <i>"Keep your friends close, keep your enemies closer."</i> is what they say, right?...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I am going to sell you as a pleasure slave to a man I despise."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394164ra/758870.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You're entire life is going to change. You should try to accept that, because there's no possible way to avoid it. Like it or not, fight it or don't, your old life is over."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>So, as I started reading this, I thought to myself: <i>"How could I possibly "enjoy" reading a story like this? This is just too messed up for words..."</i>.And how shocking as it may seem, I did enjoy reading it in the end. The story kept me on the edge of my seet the entire time. It managed to grasp my attention from the very first page till the very last one... <br><br>It was tough to read a lot of the things that Olivia/Livvie had to go through, but the author really managed to add a very human, relatable side to it all. It also helped that the book was written in a dual POV (Livvie's side in first person; Caleb's in third person), so we get a good idea of what was going in both Caleb and Livvie's head and how their feelings were constantly developing throughout the story. To me, that made it a lot easier to relate to Caleb; it showed that he wasn't just a monster after all. His past is what made him the man he's become today, but it's his present that keeps defining what kind of a person he is behind the dark facade...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"He was my tormentor and my solace; the creator of the dark and the light within."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And Livvie, I really admired her strength throughout the entire story. She was a survivor, who tried to stand up for herself as much as possible. And after a while she started to develop feelings towards her captor, but given the circumstances I think her feelings were perfectly understandable...Caleb was a master manipulator. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Caleb was a strange person, cruel and inhuman; a monster, but at other times, he seemed so capable of something like caring. He made me cry and scream and shake with fear, and nearly a split second later he could make me almost believe he wasn't responsible for any of it."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The ending was both comforting and frustrating as hell, because it left me with a lot of questions and it made me want to read the second book <u>right away!!!</u> And after reading the first chapter of <i>Seduced In The Dark, I already have even more questions...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Caleb can't be dead, right??? Did he really die while trying to protect Livvie from Rafiq?? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> </i><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/421444.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p>I NEED ANSWERS!!!<br><br><br><b>4.5 DARKLY CAPTIVATING STARS!!!</b><br>(I'm giving this one 4.5 stars instead of 5 because I've heard that the second one is even better so there's still a little room for improvement...)<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2630996574946249186" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_536344133" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536344133" />
    <a title="Dd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9444787-dd"><img alt="Dd" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536344133?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dd" href="/user/show/9444787-dd">Dd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536344133" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12894626829874780499"><br/><b>
  <i>He was the monster that no one thought to look for in the light of day.....</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/><i>And she....</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She was the instrument of his revenge,<br/>His way of reaching his mark.<br/>His Kitten,<br/>His captive in the dark.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><br/><i>Like a falcon,she needed the dark to understand who her master was.</i><br/><br/>----------------------------------------------------------<br/><br/><b>Caleb --</b><br/><br/>He was kidnapped very young and sold to slavery.He had to face things which will make hardened men shudder.<br/><br/>But he was a survivor.Somehow he survived till he was re</span>
  <span id="freeText12894626829874780499" style="display:none"><br /><b>
  <i>He was the monster that no one thought to look for in the light of day.....</i>
</b><br /><br /><br /><i>And she....</i><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She was the instrument of his revenge,<br />His way of reaching his mark.<br />His Kitten,<br />His captive in the dark.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><br /><i>Like a falcon,she needed the dark to understand who her master was.</i><br /><br />----------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>Caleb --</b><br /><br />He was kidnapped very young and sold to slavery.He had to face things which will make hardened men shudder.<br /><br />But he was a survivor.Somehow he survived till he was rescued.<br /><br />And after that,he dedicated his life to vengeance.<br /><br /><br /><i>Now,to be completely fair.....</i><br /><br />I was not expecting a Prince Charming.And neither did I get one.<br /><br /><br /><b>"You're not a damsel in distress and I'm not the handsome prince come to save you."</b><br /><br /><br />I was not expecting kindness or any other soft feelings in Caleb.They had long been beaten and raped out of him.<br /><br />But that does not mean that I condone what he did.<br /><br />Blind in his lust for vengeance,he was doing exactly what was done to him years ago......<br /><br /><br /><b>There was only one obstacle remaining between him and vengeance.The last true test of his soullessness--<br /><br />willfully stripping someone of their freedom.</b><br /><br /><br />But,what I liked was that somehow,by passing the last test of soullessness,he got something resembling his soul back.<br /><br /><br /><b>Livvie --</b><br /><br />There were many reasons for her being chosen.<br />Poor,beautiful,submissive,...and a survivor.<br /><br />So she became Kitten.But this Kitten had claws.<br /><br /><br /><b>"I hate you!" I roared. "I hate you, you horrible son of a bitch."</b><br /><br /><br />She tried to hate him.But we are strange creatures.Bereft of warmth and kindness,we seek it from any source we can.So did she.And she soaked it up when Caleb showered her with kindness.<br /><br />Most of the story was written from her point of view.And the turmoil inside her was quite apparent.<br /><br /><br /><b>He was my tormentor and my solace; the creator of the dark and the light within.</b><br /><br /><br />Yes.That he was.He was cruel and ruthless....a monster.And she feared him the most when he showed that there was some spark of humanity left inside the monster.<br /><br /><br /><b>I abruptly feared his kindness more than his cruelty.</b><br /><br />----------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Well,well,well,...now we reach the controversial part!!!</i>
</b><br /><br />As we all know,this book is highly controversial.Most of my friends were enthralled by this book and a few were disgusted.<br /><br />I was neither.<br /><br />The reason I gave it 4 stars is because I appreciate the great execution and unique concept of this story.<br /><br />I liked it.<br /><br />Though I am feeling a bit peeved that it failed to evoke in me the strong feelings it did in others.<br /><br /><br /><i>Anyway,here goes...</i><br /><br /><u>Warning- Minor spoilers ahead!!!</u><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Caleb is cold,unfeeling,cruel,....monster? Will I call him a monster?</i>
</b><br /><br />I do not know.Maybe.<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>Were the things he did justified because of his past?</b>
</i><br /><br />No.Absolutely not.<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>Is he evil though?</b>
</i><br /><br />I do not think so.Any evil person would have enjoyed the plight of Livvie.Would have enjoyed hurting Livvie.<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>Did he enjoy hurting her?</b>
</i><br /><br />No.<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>She awakens in him a bit of humanity.She becomes to him more than an instrument.Still,he is willing to let her face a fate worse than death.Does that make it better or worse?</b>
</i><br /><br />Again,I do not know.And I won't know till I read the next part of the duet.<br /><br /><br /><b>Because I have to see what he decides.I have to see what he chooses.</b><br /><br /><br /><b>That's all for now,Readers.<br /><br />Ta-Ta!!</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12894626829874780499" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer447828964" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5749306708161131793"><b>
  <i>Whatever your little school-girl brain told you about men is absurdly wrong. This isn’t a romance. You’re not a damsel in distress and I’m not the handsome prince come to save you. You ran. I went to collect my property. End of story.</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/><b>Caleb</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407543i/796079._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='547' alt='ass' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Wow!! This was a Very Wicked Tasty Treat!! Sexy, Dark, and Erotic!!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>He didn’t feel guilt very often and she seemed to have an uncanny ability to bring it out of him. The feeling was…alien, unpleasant, and aggravating as hell.</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/>Unfortunately, Caleb is the b</span>
  <span id="freeText5749306708161131793" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Whatever your little school-girl brain told you about men is absurdly wrong. This isn’t a romance. You’re not a damsel in distress and I’m not the handsome prince come to save you. You ran. I went to collect my property. End of story.</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>Caleb</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407543i/796079._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="547" alt="ass" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Wow!! This was a Very Wicked Tasty Treat!! Sexy, Dark, and Erotic!!<br><br><b>
  <i>He didn’t feel guilt very often and she seemed to have an uncanny ability to bring it out of him. The feeling was…alien, unpleasant, and aggravating as hell.</i>
</b><br><br><br>Unfortunately, Caleb is the bad guy in this love story. He's on a mission of revenge and an innocent love slave is to be his tool. She is beautiful and shy and he intends to abduct her.<br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386318350ra/7337223.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="victim" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>This book isn't all black and white. There are a lot of grey areas. It will make you curse and wanna throw things!! This author does a wonderful job of making you dislike Caleb, but not so much that you can't pull for him to find redemption. I loved the alternating points of view from Caleb and from his Pet, Kitten.<br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>He guessed she no longer thought he was cute. Good. Cute was for pussies...</i>
</b><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405114025i/10344478._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="266" alt="Caleb" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>He is the most beautiful thing I have ever seen, that includes puppies, babies, rainbows, sunsets, and sunrises. I can’t even call him a man – men don’t look this good. His skin is beautifully tanned, as if the sun itself took the time to kiss his skin to perfection. His muscled forearms are dusted with the same golden hair of his head. And his eyes mimic the blue-green of the Caribbean Sea I’ve only seen on movie posters.</i>
</b><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416124742i/11895156.jpg" width="400" height="266" alt="d" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Kitten has been abducted by the most beautiful thing she has ever seen. How can something so perfect on the outside be so fucked up and dark on the inside. How can someone so wrong make her feel such intense lust!!! The chemistry between these two is INSANE!! Unfortunately, Caleb comes across a little insane, as he struggles with an internal battle. He begins to want something that he can never have!! What happens when a man becomes obsessed with his captive?<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415676578i/11828218.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="d" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Only women were capable of being so fucking sexy you wanted to lick them clean when they considered themselves dirty. </i>
</b><br><br><br>I don't tend to like heroines that cry and or blush a lot. But I was able to tolerate Kitten because she was truly innocent. She was also beautiful enough to tempt men, but young and shy enough that she tried to hide it in order to avoid unwanted attention.<br><br><br>I can only recommend this book to lovers of Dark Erotica. This book involves violence, abduction, and rape. The subject matter revolves around human trafficking and the author represents it in a realistic manner. Caleb is no saint, but he definitely isn't the devil. The character development is believable and well thought out. I immensely enjoyed this book and could not wait to dive into the sequel!!<br><br><br><b>My Dark Duet Reviews:<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/447829073" rel="nofollow noopener">Seduced in the Dark</a><br></b></span>

<div id="review_960220357" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/960220357" />
    <a title="Stylo Fantome" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32061247-stylo-fantome"><img alt="Stylo Fantome" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555440753p2/32061247.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/960220357?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stylo Fantome" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stylo Fantome" href="/user/show/32061247-stylo-fantome">Stylo Fantome</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12541075-captive-in-the-dark">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32061247-stylo-fantome?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer960220357" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8940224406340588888">I think this story was amazing. Stockholm syndrome, love, seduction, whatever. Kitten and Caleb have a truly unique relationship. He is an anti-hero. Or an anti-villain? Something. I have read this series many times, and my thoughts change on it each time. This is totally cheesy, but I think fate brings people together, and hey, maybe this was fate's way of bringing them together. A horrific, traumatizing way of doing so - but we can't all have a The Notebook kind of relationship.<br/><br/>I don't think t</span>
  <span id="freeText8940224406340588888" style="display:none">I think this story was amazing. Stockholm syndrome, love, seduction, whatever. Kitten and Caleb have a truly unique relationship. He is an anti-hero. Or an anti-villain? Something. I have read this series many times, and my thoughts change on it each time. This is totally cheesy, but I think fate brings people together, and hey, maybe this was fate's way of bringing them together. A horrific, traumatizing way of doing so - but we can't all have a The Notebook kind of relationship.<br /><br />I don't think this "glorifies" the sex slave trade - if you've read it, it makes it look absolutely terrifying. It's a BOOK. It's FANTASY. Getting upset over what this book is about is like those people who are against Harry Potter because it glorifies the occult and Satanism. AKA, STUPID. Because YOU don't like it, it shouldn't be written? And therefore deserves to be bullied and censored? Who are these people, who feel they have the right to tell us all what we should, or shouldn't, be reading and writing? I didn't realize there were rules.<br /><br />I think leaving a bad review because you didn't understand something, or because it's not your preferred genre, is completely unfair. If you don't like to read horror, would you go out and read Stephen King and then give him a one star and scathingly horrible review? What a silly waste of time.<br /><br />Now, if you like Dark Taboo Erotica, and you just didn't care for the story or voice or writing style, then that is understandable. Except with this story, because all those things were perfect.<br /><br />Read this book. Unless you don't like dark, twisted, mind-fuckery. Then don't read it. But you are missing out, because it's amazing. There were parts that made me cry. Parts that made my heart race. Parts that made it break completely. Parts that I read over and over again. Definitely a fave.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_356551106" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/356551106" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/356551106?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Stacia (the 2010 club) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4136444-carina">Carina </a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=dark-or-taboo">dark-or-taboo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=romantica-or-erotica">romantica-or-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=bdsm-or-person-in-control">bdsm-or-person-in-control</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer356551106" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16462708247182021924"><i>Adult review for dark/taboo erotic content</i><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He was my tormentor and my solace, the creator of the dark and the light within.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>Livvie has been taken for reasons she doesn't understand. She is held and tortured in a dark room, given little to no information other than being told to obey if she wants to avoid further punishment. She is stripped bare to her very soul, left with nothing to cling to except for the shred of mercy that her abusive captor seems to display in very brief flashes.<br/><blockquote>
 </blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16462708247182021924" style="display:none"><i>Adult review for dark/taboo erotic content</i><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He was my tormentor and my solace, the creator of the dark and the light within.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Livvie has been taken for reasons she doesn't understand. She is held and tortured in a dark room, given little to no information other than being told to obey if she wants to avoid further punishment. She is stripped bare to her very soul, left with nothing to cling to except for the shred of mercy that her abusive captor seems to display in very brief flashes.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I needed to get out of here before I lost my mind.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />How long does it take for one person to crack? How long does it take for an already exhausted human being to give in to the idea of staying a captive forever, rather than continuing to fight for their freedom? How long would it take for a person to find comfort in the arms of the one person who might be the end of them?<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I let him. I was always seeking shelter in the people who hurt me the most. My mother. My father. Caleb. Like a battered dog begging for love from a malicious master. It was all I knew.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />This is not a romance. This story is meant to make you think. Make NO mistake with the interpretation. Just because you may or may not find yourself feeling compassion for Caleb the broken anti-hero, this does not make the story a romance. This is dark &amp; taboo erotica.<br /><br />This book is MEANT to be a psychological mind-fuck. Period. If you pick up <i>Captive in the Dark</i> and find yourself disgusted enough to want to write a ranty review about how wrong everything is, you are probably missing the point of the book. I will write it again : This NOT a romance. Here, I'll even let the book text even spell it out for you...<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Whatever your little school-girl brain told you about men is absurdly wrong. This isn't a romance. You're not a damsel in distress and I'm not the handsome prince come to rescue you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><b>What this book is :</b><br /><br />Scary<br />Disturbing<br />Thought-provoking<br />Sensual in parts (whether or not you want to comply with where it goes)<br /><br /><b>What this book made me feel :</b><br /><br />Sadness<br />Frustration<br />Confusion<br />Worry that I might want something I shouldn't<br /><br /><b>Are we allowed to root for Caleb and Livvie as a couple if this situation is completely wrong?</b><br /><br />That's the beauty of books. Everyone gets to want what they want. Maybe you want to see Caleb get a bullet in his head for what he's done. Maybe you want to see Caleb and Livvie find understanding in each other. I think even the people who might be pulling for C&amp;L to come together will be the first to admit that the situation is warped in every way. There is no way to romanticize what has happened.<br /><br /><b>Am I rooting for these two people to become a couple?</b><br /><br />I'm not ready to figure out what I want to happen. Yet.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16462708247182021924" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1344009217" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1344009217" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1344009217?book_show_action=true">Jul 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780615429502" href="/book/show/12649641-captive-in-the-dark">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=smexy-read">smexy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=sobfest">sobfest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=mind-blown">mind-blown</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=highly-recommended-na">highly-recommended-na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=smut-smut-smut">smut-smut-smut</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1344009217" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5394528355007330642"><i>
  <b>"While I slept, he had made himself the master of my fate, and I could do nothing but allow it."</b>
</i> <br/><br/>Holy smokes! What have I just read?<br/><br/>My reactions throughout the book:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432357490ra/14945105.gif' width='250' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439421543ra/15835585.gif' width='250' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439420597ra/15835435.gif' width='250' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12513614.Captive_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___1_' title='Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts' rel='nofollow noopener'>Captive in the Dark</a> surprised me to no end! It's one of those books that can make me pause for a while, contemplate and question myself if I'm still <b>normal</b>? Because it's the kind of book that I shouldn't love, but I did. It's <b>dark</b>, <b>twisted</b>, and full of <b>fuckeries</b>, and yet... I love it! <br/><br/>This book is not your typical romance book. I</span>
  <span id="freeText5394528355007330642" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"While I slept, he had made himself the master of my fate, and I could do nothing but allow it."</b>
</i> <br><br>Holy smokes! What have I just read?<br><br>My reactions throughout the book:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432357490ra/14945105.gif" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439421543ra/15835585.gif" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439420597ra/15835435.gif" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12513614.Captive_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___1_" title="Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive in the Dark</a> surprised me to no end! It's one of those books that can make me pause for a while, contemplate and question myself if I'm still <b>normal</b>? Because it's the kind of book that I shouldn't love, but I did. It's <b>dark</b>, <b>twisted</b>, and full of <b>fuckeries</b>, and yet... I love it! <br><br>This book is not your typical romance book. It's not even about kidnap books that happen in some mushy, romantic movies. Nope. It's abduction with cruelty-- a book where a captor inflicts pain to his captive for the sake of escaping his traumatic past and sort of relieving his inner torment.<br><br>The story opens with an introduction of the main character <b>Caleb</b> who had a very complicated and painful past. He grew up with an absolute desire for revenge to someone whose influence and wealth are infinite. By operating a sex slave business, his mission to find connection to that someone and give revenge is already too close. Until he met the innocent and fragile <b>Olivia</b>, the perfect prospect for a sex slave, and things began to take place.<br><br>This book is quite <b>disturbing</b> but there's something powerful about it that captivated me from the first page up to the last. It might be because of Caleb. Because no matter how much I try to hate him for his twisted personality, I still found myself drawn to him. The empathy I felt for him is indescribable I thought I might be having Stockholm Syndrome. All throughout the book I basically wanted to read more and find out what made him do things like what he did to Olivia and what made him become a monster. <br><br>When it comes to Olivia, she is a perfectly imperfect character. I found her too soft in the beginning. I did not like the way she always react by crying and sobbing. She could do better than that. Thankfully, her character improved in the middle portion of the book and she became tough, unyielding, and admirable.<br><br>Despite how this book appeared to be disturbing, it was well-done. The way it was written by the author is impressive. The storyline and the plot were greatly executed. It's also <b>fast-paced</b> and <b>totally compelling</b> and there were also action and thrilling scenes that are bone-chilling. I also love the <b>romance</b> in this book. It's deep and stirring.<br><br>My emotions all throughout the book can't be explained. This novel is absolutely a masterpiece! I can't wait to find out what happens in the next book!<br><br>Rating: 5 Captivating Stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="5394528355007330642" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1000311649" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1000311649" />
    <a title="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14717996-kainat-hufflepuff-proud"><img alt="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517124730p2/14717996.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1000311649?book_show_action=true">Jul 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" href="/user/show/14717996-kainat-hufflepuff-proud">Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1000311649" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9820147421731884674"><b>
  <i>“This isn't a romance.<br/><br/> You're not a damsel in distress,<br/><br/>and I'm not the handsome prince come to save you.”<i></i></i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389927i/751308._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><u>If you are looking for a good girl/ bad boy romance, this book is not for you; you've been warned.</u> So please don't try to pin this on me if you ended up not enjoying it. I am not recommending this to anyone, read at your own risk. Here, i'm admitting it, this book is downright fucked up. <br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431366ra/865531.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First of all, you need to decide if you want to look at it as Olivia's story or Caleb's story. It's w</span>
  <span id="freeText9820147421731884674" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“This isn't a romance.<br><br> You're not a damsel in distress,<br><br>and I'm not the handsome prince come to save you.”<i></i></i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389927i/751308._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>If you are looking for a good girl/ bad boy romance, this book is not for you; you've been warned.</u> So please don't try to pin this on me if you ended up not enjoying it. I am not recommending this to anyone, read at your own risk. Here, i'm admitting it, this book is downright fucked up. <br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431366ra/865531.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First of all, you need to decide if you want to look at it as Olivia's story or Caleb's story. It's written in first person, Olivia's POV, but we get to see Caleb's thoughts as well. <br><br><b>
  <i>"There was only one obstacle <br><br>remaining between him and vengeance. <br><br>The last true test of his soullessness—willfully <br><br>stripping someone of their freedom."</i>
</b><br><br>Caleb was abducted from his home and sold into slavery when he was a child by a mobster. Later a man named Rafiq rescued him, now they are both hell bend on revenge on the same man. If Caleb is to get close enough to strike, he must become the very thing he abhors. His plan is to kidnap a beautiful poor girl, who no one will miss, and train her as a "pleasure" slave to get close to his target.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439421543ra/15835585.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"The girl scrambled into his lap and buried her face in his shirt. <br><br>Against his chest, her frantic, <br><br>pleading sobs vibrated his entire body. <br><br>Was she using him as protection?"</i>
</b><br><br>As you may have guessed, Olivia starts to get Stockholm Syndrome. Keep in mind, this is the girl who's family doesn't even love her, she never had many friends, her life hadn't even started before she got sucked into Caleb's lala land. She starts feeling a connection with Caleb, and that was the saddest part of the story! I wanted her to run away, but at the same time i wanted her to stay. You are going through everything with her, at this point the book starts to mess with your mind. You can't even make up your mind about what's right, or what you are feeling. It's such a dark read!! <br><br><i>
  <b>“Dealing with Caleb was all about perspective. <br><br>You couldn’t appreciate his kindness until you’d felt his cruelty.” </b>
</i><br><br>Do I love Caleb? Yasss!!! God, I know I shouldn't, but I do!! But that does not mean I didn't want to stab him in the face sometimes. I'm speechless.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465437388ra/19355635.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <span id="freeText5228431115835180236" style="display:none">Okay so it is the longest review in the history😑 <br>Contains in between 6,000-7,000 characters<br>IDK who will be interested to read the whole damn thing 😂 <br>In my defense I was overwhelmed and needed to get it out of my system.So I wrote an essay yayy 🤐😑<br>( My teachers would be damn proud ,you bet huh 😂)<br><br><b>Part 1- September 07, 2020- THE REVIEW (the big guy)<br>Part 2- September 06, 2020- Little rant about finally starting the book<br>Part 3- September 03, 2020- The bigger rant -My History with the book</b><br><br><br><u>Update 7 September ,2020<br>Finally done with the book and I've a lot to say ❤</u><br>So here it goes-<br><br><br><b>"Just do me one favor and don’t...I don’t want to die slow.”</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1599468834i/30073287.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>An hour have been passed I am like still shaking from reading chapter 12.<br><br>First I want to ask myself<br>"Girl !!! what took you so dang long?"<br>I don't understand why the book's Genre is Dark Romance I would say It's a Psychological Thriller and it is not even my genre but I loveeeeed it.<br><br>I'll categorise my review in four parts<br>1. Caleb<br>2. Olivia<br>3. Plot <br>4. Why do I want to read the rest of the series<br><br><br>**********I'll putting my whole perspective on Caleb out there so it might get little spoilerish , so you may want to ignore his part************<br><br><br><b>Caleb</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1599468966i/30073290._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lets talk about my insecurity before stating my thoughts on Caleb<br><br>Before starting the book I thought I would symphatise or justify Caleb. That I would catch some sort of stockholm syndrome<br>But that wasn’t my case thankfully it was quite the opposite.<br><br>I should have know better. <br>Sugar coating crime doesn’t agree with me. <br><br><b>SUGAR COATING ABUSE IN THE NAME OF PLEASURE WITHOUT CONSENT OF THE OPPOSITE PARTY DOESN'T AGREE WITH ME!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!</b><br><br>No matter what the reason is Crime is Crime. <br><br>Just because someone had a horrible past that doesn’t justify he would give the same treatment to others.<br><br>Sorry I can't sympathise a psychopath.<br><br>Caleb ,He needs urgent treatment. He doesn’t even qualify as a mobster. <br>He is sick and in need of medication. The wires in his head had been broken long ago. <br>He had lost his consince. He is beyond repair.<br><br><b>But here is the twist and the page turner</b><br><br>Caleb has never been touched with loving hands.<br>My heart ached so bad because he was "Master Caleb" not a random "normal Caleb".<br><br>I wanted to love him<br>My heart wanted to love a man who probably never been touched other than from misters or mistresses or criminal out of lust or hatred .<br><br><u>To me Caleb is a Virgin in this way</u><br><br><b>And that's the mind fuckery of the book. There is a really thin silver lining between Master Caleb and the Lover Caleb. From the beginning till the very last of the book it is a constant battle of mind <br>that-<br>Do u want to HOLD his hand <br>or <br>Do u want to CUT his hand</b><br><br><br><b>Olivia</b><br>Unpopular opinion <br>to me She is the show stopper of the book.<br>I couldn't put down the book. I was just digging deep and deep because of her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1599468834i/30073288._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I momentarily forgot who am I. Suddenly I was seeing myself in Olivia's position .<br>I was Olivia.<br>IDK how to say it ; it felt like I was living the life of Olivia.<br>I was going through the torments with her. Her bravery, courage , calm amazed me . <br><br><u>She is soft yet strong<br>She is Kitten yet the Lioness</u><br><br><br><b>Plot</b><br><br>Straight out <br>It is about Human Trafficking and pleasure slavery<br><br>Triggers I found<br>●Rape and Attempt to rape <br>●All sort of Abuse<br>●Physical violation<br><br>P.S-If you have seen enough crime shows in your life I believe you will be able to endure it because all of my triggers and nightmares were there still I couldn't stop reading.<br><br><b>4.Why I'll be reading rest of the series</b><br><br>a) I am dying to know if there will be a Character development phase for Caleb ( is it even possible for someone like him) <br>For all I know Man could have been a serial killer 😑<br><br>b)Olivia ,What will happen to her ?Will she be rescued ? Will her family accept her?<br><br>c)Most importantly what happens to "them" <br>Is there even a them <br>or it is Just Master and His pet<br><br>So yeah without any doubt I am proceeding forward <br>Totally on board.<br><br><i>Note: Is it just me or the cover of the book is hideous 😂 and scary as **** not even exaggerating I even had a nightmare about the cover. I think first impression is the last impression and the cover really made me apprehensive about the book at the first place 😂</i><br><br><br><br><br><b>Update- 6 September, 2020 -Currently Reading</b> <br><br>It is official!!!<br>It is happening!!!!<br>Finally I have stopped acting like a Chicken <br>And I have started the book already 30 Pages in 🤐<br>I'll keep y'all posted hopefully<br> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1599398935ra/30070294.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><u>03 September, 2020</u><br><br><b>"A brief history of Yeasmin Alo and Captivate in the Dark ft My Shenanigans"</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1599192140ra/30058779.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>(my advance apologizes to whoever going to endure my childish Rambling. I am sorry 😑 I am ashamed trust me )</i><br><br>So here it goes-<br><br>From Last 2 or 3 months I have been looking for Dark Romance.<br>From My research and from my friends recommendations I got to know about this book. So I added it to my TBR.<br>I also got to know It was one of the most intense Dark romance book out there and at that time I've not read any Dark books so I thought of taking a Rain check and start with another "Semi Dark " book before jumping into any "Intense Dark" stuffs.<br><br>That said Semi Dark book I hated it so much 😑😑<br>You may ask which book you are talking about ?<br>It is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24235463.Three__Two__One_321_" title="Three, Two, One 321  by J.A. Huss" rel="nofollow noopener">Three, Two, One 321 </a><br><br>Lots of my friends liked it too. and I totally respect that and understood it might not be my "cup of tea"<br><br>It takes a lot for me to actually hate a book. So afterwards I thought If I couldn't digest <b>Three, Two, One</b> how am I going to read <br>this one . So I removed it from my TBR<br><br>Then L.J Shen happened. After reading all the taboo stuffs , heart breaks from L.J's books and Loving it soooooo much ,now I actually want to give this book a fair chance.<br><br>Not right now but<br>Soon ❤<br>I think it will be worth to take a risk. I also have never DNF any book 😅 so I would just do that if it gets too much that's what I am telling myself.<br>"DNF if you don't like it"<br><br>P.S- If I want to run for the hills after reading this then it is even better ☺ And I am Game . I could use some Cardio 😏.</span>

<div id="review_436012881" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/436012881" />
    <a title="Bayli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6979410-bayli"><img alt="Bayli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498671323p2/6979410.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/436012881?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bayli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bayli" href="/user/show/6979410-bayli">Bayli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6979410-bayli?shelf=tbr-that-i-own">tbr-that-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6979410-bayli?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6979410-bayli?shelf=must-read-soon">must-read-soon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6979410-bayli?shelf=romance-adult">romance-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6979410-bayli?shelf=i-want-to-punch-things">i-want-to-punch-things</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6979410-bayli?shelf=yes-it-made-me-cry">yes-it-made-me-cry</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer436012881" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12518252122503598049"><b>Okay. I need to breathe for a second. Sort out my thoughts. Try and figure out what to make of this jumble of emotions I am feeling right now...</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394599ra/759738.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>5 Stars. It was sadistic.... it was traumatizing.... it was down right painful to read... But god, I loved it. Damn it all, I freakin loved this book.</i>
</b><br/><br/>My first thought after finishing up this gripping story: <i>Is there something seriously wrong with me? Why would I actually enjoy reading this book? Why do I think this is now going straight to my "favori</i></span>
  <span id="freeText12518252122503598049" style="display:none"><b>Okay. I need to breathe for a second. Sort out my thoughts. Try and figure out what to make of this jumble of emotions I am feeling right now...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394599ra/759738.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>5 Stars. It was sadistic.... it was traumatizing.... it was down right painful to read... But god, I loved it. Damn it all, I freakin loved this book.</i>
</b><br><br>My first thought after finishing up this gripping story: <i>Is there something seriously wrong with me? Why would I actually enjoy reading this book? Why do I think this is now going straight to my "favorites" book shelf? Is my brain not working correctly? How could I possibly give this book 5 stars after seriously wanting to chuck my kindle across the room?.</i> <br><br>Well, I don't know if there is something seriously wrong with me... All I know is that this book captivated me from the very beginning to very end. <br><br><b>
  <i>He was the monster that no one thought to look for in the light of day. It was a common mistake. People often believed they were safer in the light, thinking monsters only came out at night. But safety - like light - is a facade. Underneath, the whole world is drenched in darkness.</i>
</b><br><br>Meet the gorgeous daylight monster, Caleb (Keleb, "Dog"). He didn't look like the type of man a girl should fear. In fact, to Livvie- he was salvation. He was the man she ran to when another was seeking to cause her harm. That's how she met Caleb. Running away from a stalking man and throwing herself into the arms of another. Throwing herself into what she didn't know at the time- was simply another predator. <br><br>Caleb new he needed a pretty American girl. They were were the most desirable and he needed the best if he was going to get to the man he was destined to kill- the man he had been waiting and trained to kill since he was just a young boy. He knew that this girl, Livvie, or as he likes to call her "Kitten" would be perfect for his needs.<br><br><b>
  <i>He had chosen a beautiful submissive. And what was a submissive if not adaptable - if not a survivor?</i>
</b><br><br>Meet Livvie. Livvie has had a rough life. A mother that doesn't love her and insists that Livvie is a whore. A father that is no longer around and the memories that she does have are all hurtful. She has a number of brothers and sisters- she is seemingly not close to any of them. All she can do is try to survive, try to make her mother love her- try to prove to herself that she is not a <b>whore.</b><br><br>That's when she's captured by the very man she has been fantasizing about since she ran into him. Believing that he was one of the good guys- only to find out he's from her very worst nightmare.<br><br>Yet is he?<br><br>Livvie seems to be two different people. She's strong and feisty yet at times she's shy and submissive. When she just can't take any more- she lashes out becoming more like a lion than the "kitten" name her captive has given her.<br><br>It would seem as if Livvie can't be broken- yet that's exactly what Caleb needs from her. He needs to break her down. He needs her to give into his every command. He needs her to do without question, to stop fighting him. But it's against her nature to allow herself to become this for him... Will she? Will she be what Caleb needs her to be?<br><br>Kitten and the Dog... How fitting are those names? They seem to go together dont they? But do they really? Are those two animals not opposites? Or do those two things belong together? They are both animals. Not humans. <b>No no, not humans. </b><br><br>A dog can be trained to attack. A dog can be trained to kill under command. A dog can be viscous if not loved and cared for. Is this was Caleb has become? Has he become the name that his capture had given him?<br><br>Kittens... Small dainty little things.. Mewing when upset or hurt, purring when happy and content. Kittens are sweet, docile creatures. When faced against a dog- would they ever stand a chance? Sure they have nails- they can lash out. They can cause some harm, do a bit of damage- stand up for it's tiny self. But when it comes down to it... It's still just a small, innocent animal. In the end the kitten would lose the fight against the dog. Is this Livvie. Is she now exactly what her capture has named her... a Kitten. <br><br>That's Caleb and Livvie's relationship. Cat vs Dog. <br><br>The relationship between the two is obviously confusing. At the beginning Livvie runs to him for safety! Even after she's been captured by him- she still seeks his arms when other men threaten her. She wants Calebs arms wrapped around her. <br><br>There are times where Caleb does things to her that just make you want to jump into this book and strangle is psychotic ass... He does things that are humiliating, painful, and all around frightening. <br><br>There were times I felt like I was Livvie... I felt trapped, i couldnt move, I couldnt breathe, couldnt speak... Because if she did she would be punished and there was absolutely nothing she nor I could do about it... So, I did the only thing I could possibly do in this situation- I continued to read. <br><br>*******************************<br><b>My final thoughts</b><br>This book made me uncomfortable. It was dark, horrific, challenging, and dangerous. It was disgusting and disturbing. It pissed me off. <br><br>I don't like Caleb. <br>His past now dictates who he is- and that bothers me. He knows what he is doing to Livvie is going to break her soul. He knows this because he has experiences it. He knows what it's like to be humiliated time after time... To have your choices chosen FOR you. He knows what it's like to be beaten. He knows what it's like to be sold to man after man for sex. He knows all of this- has feelings for Livvie, yet he still plans on going through with selling her to the worst of them all?<br><br>I hate him. <br><br><b>I may go back and edit this review in a few days when I've had more time to process</b><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12518252122503598049" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_250500261" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/250500261" />
    <a title="Rhonda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3078175-rhonda"><img alt="Rhonda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1391830542p2/3078175.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/250500261?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rhonda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rhonda" href="/user/show/3078175-rhonda">Rhonda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3078175-rhonda?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3078175-rhonda?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3078175-rhonda?shelf=swoonworthy-anti-hero">swoonworthy-anti-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer250500261" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2997078969463948618"><i>Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet #1)<br/>By C.J. Roberts</i><br/><b>My interview with C.J. Roberts</b><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/2012/08/get-seduced-by-cj-roberts-interview-and.html?zx=6581bac8286bf70a'>http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/20...</a><br/><br/>Original Review 12-25-2011<br/><br/>I found this book while I was book shopping, and I was first attracted to the cover. I then read the blurb for the book, and while normally this is not a book I would ever choose to read, the subject matter being something I would run away screaming from, I found myself curious. I was curious how the author would pull this off. Could she make me lik</span>
  <span id="freeText2997078969463948618" style="display:none"><i>Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet #1)<br />By C.J. Roberts</i><br /><b>My interview with C.J. Roberts</b><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/2012/08/get-seduced-by-cj-roberts-interview-and.html?zx=6581bac8286bf70a">http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/20...</a><br /><br />Original Review 12-25-2011<br /><br />I found this book while I was book shopping, and I was first attracted to the cover. I then read the blurb for the book, and while normally this is not a book I would ever choose to read, the subject matter being something I would run away screaming from, I found myself curious. I was curious how the author would pull this off. Could she make me like the hero? Could I really read this book? <br /><br />I knew this would be a dark story. What I wasn’t prepared for is just how dark of a place this book would take me. This is the most raw, and gritty book I have ever read. C.J. Roberts absolutely put me to the test with this one. By the time I finished this book I was too mentally exhausted to react to the ending. There were a couple of times I wasn’t sure I could continue, but I just couldn’t bring myself to put it down. The author’s writing was fantastic! The story alternates from Olivia’s 1st person POV, which puts you directly in her mind, and what is physically happening to her. Then it switches to 3rd person when Caleb’s story is being told. I had no difficulty in following the story being written this way, and in fact I loved it. It was so emotionally draining being inside Olivia’s head, but it made me understand her thought process better and relate to her. Caleb’s side of things being told in the 3rd person was perfect, because he is not the kind of guy that’s going to bear his soul for me, and I got to learn all about his heartbreaking past.<br /><br />I didn’t start out liking the hero at all, I wasn’t suppose to giving the circumstances. About halfway through, I still wasn’t so sure about him. So, did the author make me like the hero? YES she did! By the time Mrs. Roberts was finished with me, I wanted to hold Caleb and assure him everything would be okay. (Maybe I have a case of Stockholm syndrome, LOL!) Olivia and Caleb are damaged beyond repair, but I want to see them find happiness, and find a way out of the huge mess that surrounds them. Did I like this book? ABSOLUTELY!! <br /><br />I didn’t touch on the plot because the blurb tells the reader what they need to know. The story / plot was excellent, there were times I was holding my breath and didn’t realize it until I exhaled. These are my thoughts and feelings, take from it what you will. If you are thinking of reading this book, open your mind, and prepare yourself to go on a very dark journey. I was disturbed by some of the things I read, and some of the events made my heart pound, but I don’t regret a single page. C.J. Roberts has a new fan, and I can hardly wait for book 2.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2997078969463948618" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I didn’t care that he would undoubtedly hurt me at any moment…</i><br/><br/>Told in dual POV, both in 1st & 3rd person, it’s the first installment in "The Dark Duet" and it’s cliffy. At first, I couldn’t connect with Livvie’s character, I didn’t like her much but further in the story I saw her thoroughly. She was funny and shy but also fierce and brave. Oh, Caleb!   <span id="freeText7286945778237291488" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br /><br /><i>He was my tormentor and my solace; the creator of dark and the light within. I didn’t care that he would undoubtedly hurt me at any moment…</i><br /><br />Told in dual POV, both in 1st &amp; 3rd person, it’s the first installment in "The Dark Duet" and it’s cliffy. At first, I couldn’t connect with Livvie’s character, I didn’t like her much but further in the story I saw her thoroughly. She was funny and shy but also fierce and brave. Oh, Caleb! What can I say about you! There were moments that I really hated him but it couldn’t take long more than a few seconds. I wanted to hate him but I couldn’t! Yes, he was an @sshole but he also was protective of her, so attentive toward her. Loved seeing him being at war with himself, there were moments of doubting himself, of not knowing his feelings, him being confused… This was my first read by this author and I really enjoyed it! The emotion this author made me feel… Overall, loved it and hope you enjoy it as well!<br /><br />P.s I'd like to thank my dear friend, Sahar, for recommending this, you know how much I enjoyed it!</span>

<div id="review_530384701" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/530384701" />
    <a title="Tina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16458477-tina"><img alt="Tina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606198430p2/16458477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

  <span id="freeText3083978791370256689" style="display:none"><b>Abandon all hope, ye who enter here.</b><br /><br />You know what this book is about? Oh, then it gets even better. She runs away, she's captured by--wait for it--what is now a group of rapists (including a woman, guys), she's almost raped again. But wait, this time she gets it light--she's only completely bruised, some cracked ribs and cuts. You know, nothing big. And then, her initial stalker-rapist SAVES her (ohmygod, so cool, right?). And don't get started with the whole two-tormented-souls-trying-to-fight-their-pasts-and-reach-out-into-darkness-to-find-light nonsense because you just can't pull it off. There is no real story, no development, nobody gets wiser or a better person <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(but some come out raped, you know) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />You know what? I intend to buy a paperback copy of this book, just so that I can immediately recycle it and make this world a better place.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3083978791370256689" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/291456166?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexis *Reality Bites*" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites">Alexis *Reality Bites*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer291456166" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16062645603577169304">Spoiler Free Review <br/>5 STAR READ<br/>Genre: Adult Romance <br/><br/><i>'Mother. Fucker. Heat bloomed across my body. I couldn't breathe. I couldn't scream. But emotion had returned. He had tied me - naked - to a bed post. To suffer. And he was somewhere in the house fucking some whore's brains out.'</i> -Inner thoughts of Livvie in Captive in the Dark<br/><br/><b>This book rocked ALL FIVE STARS! HARD!!!</b> When i finished reading all i could say was "Whoa". Captive in the Dark starts off with two men planning revenge. Caleb and Rafiq</span>
  <span id="freeText16062645603577169304" style="display:none">Spoiler Free Review <br />5 STAR READ<br />Genre: Adult Romance <br /><br /><i>'Mother. Fucker. Heat bloomed across my body. I couldn't breathe. I couldn't scream. But emotion had returned. He had tied me - naked - to a bed post. To suffer. And he was somewhere in the house fucking some whore's brains out.'</i> -Inner thoughts of Livvie in Captive in the Dark<br /><br /><b>This book rocked ALL FIVE STARS! HARD!!!</b> When i finished reading all i could say was "Whoa". Captive in the Dark starts off with two men planning revenge. Caleb and Rafiq both seek the death of one man a billionaire by the name of Vladek Rostrovich. But first Caleb has to secure a slave. The sure way to get close to touching Vladek would be to enter a virgin slave into the Flower sale in Pakistan. Caleb has to get a girl and train her in six weeks, then make a trek across the ocean to Rafiq in the middle east.<br /><br />Well Caleb finds a girl. Livvie. With the help a Rafiq he is able to smuggle the girl to a house in mexico and begin to train her. The thing is Livvie is a fighter and as long as there is a breath in her body she will fight. <br /><br />I loved Livvie i felt everything she felt... I loved how open and honest she was with Caleb; right down to the point when she would rebel against him. She had a true "I will survive" spirit that Caleb could not beat out of her all the way to the last page.<br /><br />Now Caleb this guy has some issues. And we get glimpses into his past in the story, the guy really went through some crazy stuff at a very young age. I loved Caleb tho. And when shit hit the fan he was a not to be reckoned with. When these unknown feelings began to creep into his system for Livvie i knew it was over. Lust is one thing but love is to powerful. And once he could admit to himself thet what he was feeling for Livvie was love.... It was over i knew he would do whatever he had to do for her.<br /><br />My Ratings<br />Characters- Strong Willed and Lovable<br />Writing Style- Excellent<br />Plot/Storyline- Solid<br />Overall- <b>A MUST READ</b><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16062645603577169304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33411728-bibi?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33411728-bibi?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>
